*Sergey V. Samsonau*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: scicode-lint是一个用于检测科学Python代码中方法论错误的工具，采用两层级架构分离模式设计（构建时使用前沿模型）和执行（运行时使用小型本地模型），能够自动检测数据泄露、交叉验证错误等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 科学Python代码中的方法论错误会产生看似合理但错误的结果，传统linter和静态分析工具无法检测。随着AI生成代码的增加，对自动化方法论检查的需求日益增长。

Method: 采用两层级架构：模式设计使用前沿模型在构建时生成模式，执行使用小型本地模型在运行时检测。模式是生成的而非手动编码，适应新库版本只需token成本而非工程时间。

Result: 在Kaggle笔记本上，预处理泄露检测达到65%精确率和100%召回率；在38篇已发表论文中，精确率为62%（LLM评估）；在控制测试中，66个模式的准确率达到97.7%。

Conclusion: scicode-lint通过分离模式设计和执行的两层级架构，解决了现有ML特定linter的可持续性问题，能够有效检测科学代码中的方法论错误，适应AI生成代码的增长需求。

Abstract: Methodology bugs in scientific Python code produce plausible but incorrect results that traditional linters and static analysis tools cannot detect. Several research groups have built ML-specific linters, demonstrating that detection is feasible. Yet these tools share a sustainability problem: dependency on specific pylint or Python versions, limited packaging, and reliance on manual engineering for every new pattern. As AI-generated code increases the volume of scientific software, the need for automated methodology checking (such as detecting data leakage, incorrect cross-validation, and missing random seeds) grows. We present scicode-lint, whose two-tier architecture separates pattern design (frontier models at build time) from execution (small local model at runtime). Patterns are generated, not hand-coded; adapting to new library versions costs tokens, not engineering hours. On Kaggle notebooks with human-labeled ground truth, preprocessing leakage detection reaches 65% precision at 100% recall; on 38 published scientific papers applying AI/ML, precision is 62% (LLM-judged) with substantial variation across pattern categories; on a held-out paper set, precision is 54%. On controlled tests, scicode-lint achieves 97.7% accuracy across 66 patterns.

### [178] [In Perfect Harmony: Orchestrating Causality in Actor-Based Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17909)
*Vladyslav Mikytiv,Bernardo Toninho,Carla Ferreira*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: ACTORCHESTRA是一个用于Erlang的运行时验证框架，通过代码注入自动追踪多参与者间的因果关系，无需手动修改目标系统，并提供WALTZ规范语言来指定多参与者属性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 基于参与者的系统给运行时验证带来重大挑战：属性经常跨越多个参与者且具有复杂的因果依赖关系，非确定性的消息交错会模糊执行语义，而现有监控工具大多针对单进程行为设计。

Method: 框架通过有针对性的代码注入来检测符合OTP指南的Erlang系统，建立编排基础设施以追踪参与者间的因果关系；提供WALTZ规范语言，可自动将属性编译成可执行的Erlang监控器并与检测系统集成。

Result: 三个案例研究证明了ACTORCHESTRA在检测真实世界参与者系统中复杂行为违规方面的有效性；性能评估量化了监控基础设施的运行时开销，并分析了增加的安全保证与执行成本之间的权衡。

Conclusion: ACTORCHESTRA为Erlang的基于参与者系统提供了一个有效的运行时验证框架，能够自动追踪多参与者交互中的因果关系，并通过WALTZ语言简化多参与者属性的规范，在安全保证和执行成本之间取得了良好平衡。

Abstract: Runtime verification has gained popularity as a lightweight approach for increasing assurance in systems under scrutiny. Performing runtime checks enables dynamic monitoring and alerts for unexpected behavior, thereby improving reliability and correctness. Actor-based systems present significant challenges for runtime verification. Properties frequently span multiple actors with complex causal dependencies, while nondeterministic message interleavings can obscure execution semantics. Moreover, most existing monitoring tools are designed for single-process behavior. This paper presents ACTORCHESTRA, a runtime verification framework for Erlang that automatically tracks causality across multi-actor interactions. The framework instruments Erlang systems that comply with OTP guidelines via targeted code injection. This method establishes the orchestration infrastructure required to track causal relationships between actors without requiring manual modifications to the target system. To ease the specification of multi-actor properties, the framework provides WALTZ, a specification language that automatically compiles properties into executable Erlang monitors that integrate with the instrumented system. Three case studies demonstrate ACTORCHESTRA's effectiveness in detecting complex behavioral violations in real-world actor systems. A performance evaluation quantifies the runtime overhead of the monitoring infrastructure and analyzes the trade-offs between added safety guarantees and execution costs.

### [179] [CodeGreen: Towards Improving Precision and Portability in Software Energy Measurement](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17924)
*Saurabhsingh Rajput,Tushar Sharma*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: CodeGreen是一个模块化的软件能耗测量平台，通过解耦插桩与测量实现高精度低开销的能耗分析，支持多种编程语言和硬件平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有能耗分析工具在测量精度和开销之间存在权衡，且通常与特定硬件或编程语言紧密耦合，限制了跨平台和跨语言的能耗优化。

Method: 采用异步生产者-消费者架构解耦插桩与测量；实现原生能耗测量后端(NEMB)轮询硬件传感器；使用Tree-sitter AST查询实现自动化插桩；支持Python、C++、C、Java等多种语言。

Result: 在"Computer Language Benchmarks Game"验证中，与RAPL基准真值的相关性达到R²=0.9934，能耗-工作负载线性度达到R²=0.9997，实现了高精度测量。

Conclusion: CodeGreen通过将细粒度测量精度与跨平台可移植性相结合，为异构环境中的算法能耗优化提供了实用工具，支持多种编程语言和硬件平台。

Abstract: Accurate software energy measurement is critical for optimizing energy, yet existing profilers force a trade-off between measurement accuracy and overhead due to tight coupling with supported specific hardware or languages. We present CodeGreen, a modular energy measurement platform that decouples instrumentation from measurement via an asynchronous producer-consumer architecture. We implement a Native Energy Measurement Backend (NEMB) that polls hardware sensors (Intel RAPL, NVIDIA NVML, AMD ROCm) independently, while lightweight timestamp markers enable tunable granularity. CodeGreen leverages Tree-sitter AST queries for automated instrumentation across Python, C++, C, and Java, with straightforward extension to any Tree-sitter-supported grammar, enabling developers to target specific scopes (loops, methods, classes) without manual intervention. Validation against "Computer Language Benchmarks Game" demonstrates $R^2 = 0.9934$ correlation with RAPL ground truth and $R^2 = 0.9997$ energy-workload linearity. By bridging fine-grained measurement precision with cross-platform portability, CodeGreen enables practical algorithmic energy optimization across heterogeneous environments. Source code, video demonstration, and documentation for the tool are publicly available at: https://smart-dal.github.io/codegreen/.

Abstract: Provenance graphs model causal system-level interactions from logs, enabling anomaly detectors to learn normal behavior and detect deviations as attacks. However, existing approaches rely on brittle, manually engineered rules to build provenance graphs, lack functional context for system entities, and provide limited support for analyst investigation. We present Auto-Prov, an adaptive, end-to-end framework that leverages large language models (LLMs) to automatically construct provenance graphs from heterogeneous and evolving logs, embed system-level functional attributes into the graph, enable provenance graph-based anomaly detectors to learn from these enriched graphs, and summarize the detected attacks to assist an analyst's investigation. Auto-Prov clusters unseen log types and efficiently extracts provenance edges and entity-level information via automatically generated rules. It further infers system-level functional context for both known and previously unseen system entities using a combination of LLM inference and behavior-based estimation. Attacks detected by provenance-graph-based anomaly detectors trained on Auto-Prov's graphs are then summarized into natural-language text. We evaluate Auto-Prov with four state-of-the-art provenance graph-based detectors across diverse logs. Results show that Auto-Prov consistently enhances detection performance, generalizes across heterogeneous log formats, and produces stable, interpretable attack summaries that remain robust under system evolution.

### [181] [Security Assessment and Mitigation Strategies for Large Language Models: A Comprehensive Defensive Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17123)
*Taiwo Onitiju,Iman Vakilinia*

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大语言模型在医疗、金融等关键基础设施中广泛应用，其对抗性攻击脆弱性威胁系统完整性和用户安全。目前缺乏跨主要LLM架构的全面安全评估，导致组织无法量化风险或为敏感应用选择安全模型。

Method: 建立标准化脆弱性评估框架，对GPT-4、GPT-3.5 Turbo、Claude-3 Haiku、LLaMA-2-70B和Gemini-2.5-pro等5个广泛部署的LLM家族，使用涵盖6类攻击的10,000个对抗性提示进行系统评估，并开发多层防御系统。

Result: 评估揭示了关键安全差异，脆弱性率从11.9%到29.8%不等，表明LLM能力与安全鲁棒性不相关。开发的防御框架实现了83%的平均检测准确率，仅5%的误报率。

Conclusion: 系统化安全评估结合外部防御措施为生产环境中更安全的LLM部署提供了可行路径，证明通过标准化评估和防御框架可以有效降低对抗性攻击风险。

Abstract: Large Language Models increasingly power critical infrastructure from healthcare to finance, yet their vulnerability to adversarial manipulation threatens system integrity and user safety. Despite growing deployment, no comprehensive comparative security assessment exists across major LLM architectures, leaving organizations unable to quantify risk or select appropriately secure LLMs for sensitive applications. This research addresses this gap by establishing a standardized vulnerability assessment framework and developing a multi-layered defensive system to protect against identified threats. We systematically evaluate five widely-deployed LLM families GPT-4, GPT-3.5 Turbo, Claude-3 Haiku, LLaMA-2-70B, and Gemini-2.5-pro against 10,000 adversarial prompts spanning six attack categories. Our assessment reveals critical security disparities, with vulnerability rates ranging from 11.9\% to 29.8\%, demonstrating that LLM capability does not correlate with security robustness. To mitigate these risks, we develop a production-ready defensive framework achieving 83\% average detection accuracy with only 5\% false positives. These results demonstrate that systematic security assessment combined with external defensive measures provides a viable path toward safer LLM deployment in production environments.

### [182] [Detecting Data Poisoning in Code Generation LLMs via Black-Box, Vulnerability-Oriented Scanning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17174)
*Shenao Yan,Shimaa Ahmed,Shan Jin,Sunpreet S. Arora,Yiwei Cai,Yizhen Wang,Yuan Hong*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: CodeScan：首个针对代码生成模型的投毒扫描框架，通过分析不同干净提示下的多代代码结构相似性来检测攻击目标，准确率达97%以上


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 代码生成大语言模型在现代软件开发中日益普及，但易受后门和投毒攻击影响，现有基于令牌级生成一致性的扫描方法对源代码无效，因为相同语义可以出现在不同的语法形式中

Method: CodeScan通过分析不同干净提示下多代代码的结构相似性来识别攻击目标，结合迭代发散分析和基于抽象语法树（AST）的归一化，抽象掉表层变化并统一语义等价的代码，然后应用基于LLM的漏洞分析来确定提取的结构是否包含安全漏洞

Result: 在3种架构、多种模型大小的108个模型上评估，针对4种代表性攻击（后门和投毒设置）和3个真实世界漏洞类别，CodeScan达到97%以上的检测准确率，假阳性率显著低于先前方法

Conclusion: CodeScan是首个专门针对代码生成模型的投毒扫描框架，通过结构相似性分析有效检测攻击，为代码生成模型的安全提供了重要保障

Abstract: Code generation large language models (LLMs) are increasingly integrated into modern software development workflows. Recent work has shown that these models are vulnerable to backdoor and poisoning attacks that induce the generation of insecure code, yet effective defenses remain limited. Existing scanning approaches rely on token-level generation consistency to invert attack targets, which is ineffective for source code where identical semantics can appear in diverse syntactic forms. We present CodeScan, which, to the best of our knowledge, is the first poisoning-scanning framework tailored to code generation models. CodeScan identifies attack targets by analyzing structural similarities across multiple generations conditioned on different clean prompts. It combines iterative divergence analysis with abstract syntax tree (AST)-based normalization to abstract away surface-level variation and unify semantically equivalent code, isolating structures that recur consistently across generations. CodeScan then applies LLM-based vulnerability analysis to determine whether the extracted structures contain security vulnerabilities and flags the model as compromised when such a structure is found. We evaluate CodeScan against four representative attacks under both backdoor and poisoning settings across three real-world vulnerability classes. Experiments on 108 models spanning three architectures and multiple model sizes demonstrate 97%+ detection accuracy with substantially lower false positives than prior methods.

</details>


### [183] [LAAF: Logic-layer Automated Attack Framework A Systematic Red-Teaming Methodology for LPCI Vulnerabilities in Agentic Large Language Model Systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17239)
*Hammad Atta,Ken Huang,Kyriakos Rock Lambros,Yasir Mehmood,Zeeshan Baig,Mohamed Abdur Rahman,Manish Bhatt,M. Aziz Ul Haq,Muhammad Aatif,Nadeem Shahzad,Kamal Noor,Vineeth Sai Narajala,Hazem Ali,Jamel Abed*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: LAAF是首个针对逻辑层提示控制注入攻击的自动化红队框架，包含49种攻击技术分类和持久阶段突破器，能生成280多万种独特攻击载荷，在五个生产LLM平台上平均突破率达84%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的红队工具（如Garak、PyRIT）无法有效测试具有持久内存、RAG管道和外部工具连接的智能LLM系统面临的逻辑层提示控制注入攻击，缺乏专门的攻击技术分类和阶段递进的种子升级能力。

Method: LAAF框架包含两个核心组件：1）49种攻击技术的分类体系，涵盖编码、结构、语义、分层、触发、泄露六个类别，可跨5种变体和6个生命周期阶段组合；2）持久阶段突破器，在每阶段突破后将获胜载荷变异作为下一阶段的种子，模拟真实攻击升级过程。

Result: 在五个生产LLM平台上的三次独立测试中，LAAF的平均总突破率达到84%（范围83-86%），平台级突破率在运行间稳定在17个百分点内。分层组合和语义重构是最高效的攻击类别，分层载荷在防御良好的平台上优于编码攻击。

Conclusion: LAAF是首个专门针对逻辑层提示控制注入攻击的自动化红队框架，通过系统化的攻击技术分类和阶段递进的种子升级机制，显著提高了对智能LLM系统的安全测试效率，为防御此类攻击提供了重要工具。

Abstract: Agentic LLM systems equipped with persistent memory, RAG pipelines, and external tool connectors face a class of attacks - Logic-layer Prompt Control Injection (LPCI) - for which no automated red-teaming instrument existed. We present LAAF (Logic-layer Automated Attack Framework), the first automated red-teaming framework to combine an LPCI-specific technique taxonomy with stage-sequential seed escalation - two capabilities absent from existing tools: Garak lacks memory-persistence and cross-session triggering; PyRIT supports multi-turn testing but treats turns independently, without seeding each stage from the prior breakthrough. LAAF provides: (i) a 49-technique taxonomy spanning six attack categories (Encoding~11, Structural~8, Semantic~8, Layered~5, Trigger~12, Exfiltration~5; see Table 1), combinable across 5 variants per technique and 6 lifecycle stages, yielding a theoretical maximum of 2,822,400 unique payloads ($49 \times 5 \times 1{,}920 \times 6$; SHA-256 deduplicated at generation time); and (ii) a Persistent Stage Breaker (PSB) that drives payload mutation stage-by-stage: on each breakthrough, the PSB seeds the next stage with a mutated form of the winning payload, mirroring real adversarial escalation. Evaluation on five production LLM platforms across three independent runs demonstrates that LAAF achieves higher stage-breakthrough efficiency than single-technique random testing, with a mean aggregate breakthrough rate of 84\% (range 83--86\%) and platform-level rates stable within 17 percentage points across runs. Layered combinations and semantic reframing are the highest-effectiveness technique categories, with layered payloads outperforming encoding on well-defended platforms.

### [184] [SEAL-Tag: Self-Tag Evidence Aggregation with Probabilistic Circuits for PII-Safe Retrieval-Augmented Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17292)
*Jin Xie,Songze Li,Guang Cheng*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: SEAL-Tag是一个隐私保护的RAG运行时环境，通过验证-路由范式解决上下文泄露问题，使用SEAL-Probe协议将审计转化为结构化工具使用，生成可验证的PII证据表，并利用概率电路进行决策，显著减少自适应泄露。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检索增强生成(RAG)系统存在关键漏洞：上下文泄露，攻击者可以利用指令跟随通过自适应提取泄露个人身份信息(PII)。现有防御方法需要在语义效用和延迟之间进行僵化的权衡。

Method: 提出SEAL-Tag隐私保护运行时环境，采用验证-路由范式。引入SEAL-Probe协议，将审计转化为结构化工具使用操作，模型生成可验证的PII证据表。使用概率电路强制执行可验证的逻辑约束进行决策。为解决隐私"冷启动"问题，提出S0-S6锚定合成管道生成高保真、可溯源的RAG交互，并采用两阶段课程学习：先优化实体检测，再使模型适应严格的审计协议。

Result: 评估显示SEAL-Tag建立了新的帕累托前沿，将自适应泄露减少超过8倍，同时保持与不安全基线相当的效用和速度。

Conclusion: SEAL-Tag通过创新的验证-路由范式和结构化审计协议，有效解决了RAG系统中的上下文泄露问题，在保持高性能的同时显著增强了隐私保护能力。

Abstract: Retrieval-Augmented Generation (RAG) systems introduce a critical vulnerability: contextual leakage, where adversaries exploit instruction-following to exfiltrate Personally Identifiable Information (PII) via adaptive extraction. Current defenses force a rigid trade-off between semantic utility and latency. We present SEAL-Tag, a privacy-preserving runtime environment that resolves this via a Verify-then-Route paradigm. SEAL-Tag introduces the SEAL-Probe protocol, transforming auditing into a structured tool-use operation where the model generates a verifiable PII-Evidence Table (PET) alongside its draft. To adjudicate this evidence, we employ a Probabilistic Circuit (PC) that enforces verifiable logical constraints for robust decision-making. To overcome the privacy "Cold Start" problem, we introduce the S0--S6 Anchored Synthesis Pipeline, generating high-fidelity, provenanced RAG interactions. We pair this with a Two-Stage Curriculum that first optimizes for entity detection before aligning the model to the rigorous audit protocol. Our evaluation demonstrates that SEAL-Tag establishes a new Pareto frontier, reducing adaptive leakage by over 8$\times$ while matching the utility and speed of unsafe baselines.

*Enzo Fenoglio,Philip Treleaven*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 联邦计算系统跨越组织和司法边界时，缺乏可移植的主权约束执行机制，通常依赖运行时策略评估、共享信任基础设施或机构协议，这些方法存在协调开销大且密码学保证有限的问题。

Method: 提出联邦计算即代码（FCaC）架构，通过虚拟联邦平台（VFPs）结合核心、业务和治理合约，使用KYO、ECTs和PoP形成密码信任链，将边界准入转变为本地验证步骤而非策略决策服务。

Result: 在概念验证的跨孤岛联邦学习工作流中使用MNIST作为替代工作负载，验证了准入机制，并发布了开源实现，展示了信封签发、边界验证和信封触发的训练过程。

Conclusion: FCaC通过将宪法治理与程序治理分离，使用携带证明的能力进行本地验证，为联邦计算提供了更强的密码学保证和主权保护，同时仍支持状态服务的后准入控制。

Abstract: Federated computing (FC) enables collaborative computation such as machine learning, analytics, or data processing across distributed organizations keeping raw data local. Built on four architectural pillars, distributed data assets, federated services, standardized APIs, and decentralized services, FC supports sovereignty-preserving collaboration. However, federated systems spanning organizational and jurisdictional boundaries lack a portable mechanism for enforcing sovereignty-critical constraints. They often depend on runtime policy evaluation, shared trust infrastructure, or institutional agreements that introduce coordination overhead and provide limited cryptographic assurance. Federated Computing as Code (FCaC) is a declarative architecture that addresses this gap by compiling authority and delegation into cryptographically verifiable artifacts rather than relying on online policy interpretation. Boundary admission becomes a local verification step rather than a policy decision service. FCaC separates constitutional governance from procedural governance. Admission is validated locally at execution boundaries using proof-carrying capabilities, while stateful services may still implement post-admission controls such as ABAC, risk scoring, quotas, and workflow state. FCaC introduces Virtual Federated Platforms (VFPs), which combine Core, Business, and Governance contracts through a cryptographic trust chain: Key Your Organization (KYO), Envelope Capability Tokens (ECTs), and proof of possession (PoP). We demonstrate the approach in a proof-of-concept cross-silo federated learning workflow using MNIST as a surrogate workload to validate the admission mechanisms and release an open-source implementation showing envelope issuance, boundary verification, and envelope-triggered training.

Abstract: Function Secret Sharing (FSS) schemes enable sharing efficiently secret functions. Schemes dedicated to point functions, referred to as Distributed Point Functions (DPFs), are the center of FSS literature thanks to their numerous applications including private information retrieval, anonymous communications, and machine learning. While two-party DPFs benefit from schemes with logarithmic key sizes, multi-party DPFs have seen limited advancements: $O(\sqrt{N})$ key sizes (with $N$, the function domain size) and/or exponential factors in the key size.
  We propose a DDH-based technique reducing the key size of existing multi-party schemes. In particular, we build an honest-majority DPF with $O(\sqrt[3]{N})$ key size. Our benchmark highlights key sizes up to $10\times$ smaller (on realistic problem sizes) than state-of-the-art schemes. Finally, we extend our technique to schemes supporting comparison functions.

*De Zhang Lee,Han Fang,Ee-Chien Chang*

TL;DR: 提出基于潜在扩散模型的证明作者身份框架，通过绑定生成种子与作者身份实现比传统所有权证明更强的保障


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI生成内容（AIGC）的发展带来了知识产权保护和生成对象认证的新挑战，传统的时间戳和水印方法存在局限性，需要更强的作者身份证明机制

Method: 利用潜在扩散模型生成过程中对随机种子的控制，通过密码学伪随机函数将种子与作者身份绑定，提出包含概率裁决者的证明作者身份框架，无需任何秘密信息

Abstract: Recent advancements in AI-generated content (AIGC) have introduced new challenges in intellectual property protection and the authentication of generated objects. We focus on scenarios in which an author seeks to assert authorship of an object generated using latent diffusion models (LDMs), in the presence of adversaries who attempt to falsely claim authorship of objects they did not create. While proof-of-ownership has been studied in the context of multimedia content through techniques such as time-stamping and watermarking, these approaches face notable limitations. In contrast to traditional content creation sources (e.g., cameras), the LDM generation process offers greater control to the author. Specifically, the random seed used during generation can be deliberately chosen. By binding the seed to the author's identity using cryptographic pseudorandom functions, the author can assert to be the creator of the object. We refer to this stronger guarantee as proof-of-authorship, since only the creator of the object can legitimately claim the object. This contrasts with proof-of-ownership via time-stamping or watermarking, where any entity could potentially claim ownership of an object by being the first to timestamp or embed the watermark. We propose a proof-of-authorship framework involving a probabilistic adjudicator who quantifies the probability that a claim is false. Furthermore, unlike prior approaches, the proposed framework does not involve any secret. We explore various attack scenarios and analyze design choices using Stable Diffusion 2.1 (SD2.1) as representative case studies.

### [188] [Data Obfuscation for Secure Use of Classical Values in Quantum Computation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17725)
*Amal Raj,Vivek Balachandran*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个用于保护量子计算中经典数据的混淆技术，通过结构化量子表示和可逆操作隐藏敏感信息


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子计算中经典数据需要在可能不完全可信的环境中处理，传统加密在计算开始后保护有限，需要新的数据保护方法

Method: 将敏感数据编码到多个量子寄存器的结构化表示中，使用可逆量子操作和振幅放大技术，在不暴露底层数据的情况下选择性恢复有效编码

Result: 通过仿真评估了方法的可行性，分析了资源需求和实际限制，结果表明数据混淆可作为量子计算的补充安全原语

Conclusion: 数据混淆是保护量子计算中经典值的重要安全技术，为量子计算安全提供了新的研究方向

Abstract: Quantum computing often requires classical data to be supplied to execution environments that may not be fully trusted or isolated. While encryption protects data at rest and in transit, it provides limited protection once computation begins, when classical values are encoded into quantum registers. This paper explores data obfuscation for protecting classical values during quantum computation. To the best of our knowledge, we present the first explicit data obfuscation technique designed to protect classical values during quantum execution. We propose an obfuscation technique that encodes sensitive data into structured quantum representations across multiple registers, avoiding direct exposure while preserving computational usability. Reversible quantum operations and amplitude amplification allow selective recovery of valid encodings without revealing the underlying data. We evaluate the feasibility of the proposed method through simulation and analyze its resource requirements and practical limitations. Our results highlight data obfuscation as a complementary security primitive for quantum computing.

### [190] [Draft-and-Prune: Improving the Reliability of Auto-formalization for Logical Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17233)
*Zhiyu Ni,Zheng Liang,Liangcheng Song,Chenrui Cao,Xian Zhang,Alberto Sangiovanni-Vincentelli,Pierluigi Nuzzo*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: Draft-and-Prune (D&P)框架通过多样化和验证改进自动形式化推理，首先生成多个自然语言计划，然后筛选可执行但矛盾或模糊的形式化，最后通过多数投票聚合预测，显著提升逻辑推理性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动形式化(AF)将自然语言推理问题转换为可执行的程序，但目前AF流程脆弱：程序可能执行失败，或执行但编码错误的语义。虽然先前工作通过基于求解器反馈的修复减轻了语法失败，但减少语义失败仍然是主要瓶颈。

Method: 提出Draft-and-Prune (D&P)推理时框架：1) 草拟多个自然语言计划，并基于这些计划生成程序；2) 修剪可执行但矛盾或模糊的形式化；3) 通过多数投票聚合幸存路径的预测。

Result: 在四个基准测试(AR-LSAT、ProofWriter、PrOntoQA、LogicalDeduction)上，D&P显著增强了基于AF的推理。在AR-LSAT上，仅使用AF时，D&P在GPT-4上达到78.43%准确率，在GPT-4o上达到78.00%，显著优于最强的AF基线MAD-LOGIC和CLOVER。在其他基准测试上达到接近天花板性能，包括PrOntoQA和LogicalDeduction的100%。

Conclusion: D&P框架通过多样化和验证有效改善了自动形式化推理的鲁棒性和准确性，无需额外监督即可显著提升逻辑推理性能。

Abstract: Auto-formalization (AF) translates natural-language reasoning problems into solver-executable programs, enabling symbolic solvers to perform sound logical deduction. In practice, however, AF pipelines are currently brittle: programs may fail to execute, or execute but encode incorrect semantics. While prior work largely mitigates syntactic failures via repairs based on solver feedback, reducing semantics failures remains a major bottleneck. We propose Draft-and-Prune (D&P), an inference-time framework that improves AF-based logical reasoning via diversity and verification. D&P first drafts multiple natural-language plans and conditions program generation on them. It further prunes executable but contradictory or ambiguous formalizations, and aggregates predictions from surviving paths via majority voting. Across four representative benchmarks (AR-LSAT, ProofWriter, PrOntoQA, LogicalDeduction), D&P substantially strengthens AF-based reasoning without extra supervision. On AR-LSAT, in the AF-only setting, D&P achieves 78.43% accuracy with GPT-4 and 78.00% accuracy with GPT-4o, significantly outperforming the strongest AF baselines MAD-LOGIC and CLOVER. D&P then attains near-ceiling performance on the other benchmarks, including 100% on PrOntoQA and LogicalDeduction.

*Haozheng Luo,Yimin Wang,Jiahao Yu,Binghui Wang,Yan Chen*

TL;DR: CRAFT是一个利用模型推理能力和隐藏表示来提升对抗越狱攻击鲁棒性的红队对齐框架，通过隐藏状态空间优化实现推理级安全对齐。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: CRAFT整合对比表示学习和强化学习，分离安全和危险推理轨迹，构建支持鲁棒推理级安全对齐的潜在空间几何结构。理论证明将潜在-文本一致性融入GRPO可消除表面对齐策略。

Result: 在多个安全基准测试中，使用Qwen3-4B-Thinking和R1-Distill-Llama-8B模型，CRAFT持续优于IPO和SafeKey等最先进防御方法，推理安全性平均提升79.0%，最终响应安全性提升87.7%。

Conclusion: CRAFT通过隐藏空间推理对齐有效提升模型安全性，证明了在潜在表示层面进行安全对齐的重要性，为构建更鲁棒的AI安全防御提供了新思路。

Abstract: We propose CRAFT, a red-teaming alignment framework that leverages model reasoning capabilities and hidden representations to improve robustness against jailbreak attacks. Unlike prior defenses that operate primarily at the output level, CRAFT aligns large reasoning models to generate safety-aware reasoning traces by explicitly optimizing objectives defined over the hidden state space. Methodologically, CRAFT integrates contrastive representation learning with reinforcement learning to separate safe and unsafe reasoning trajectories, yielding a latent-space geometry that supports robust, reasoning-level safety alignment. Theoretically, we show that incorporating latent-textual consistency into GRPO eliminates superficially aligned policies by ruling them out as local optima. Empirically, we evaluate CRAFT on multiple safety benchmarks using two strong reasoning models, Qwen3-4B-Thinking and R1-Distill-Llama-8B, where it consistently outperforms state-of-the-art defenses such as IPO and SafeKey. Notably, CRAFT delivers an average 79.0% improvement in reasoning safety and 87.7% improvement in final-response safety over the base models, demonstrating the effectiveness of hidden-space reasoning alignment.

### [192] [InfoDensity: Rewarding Information-Dense Traces for Efficient Reasoning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17310)
*Chengwei Wei,Jung-jae Kim,Longyin Zhang,Shengkai Chen,Nancy F. Chen*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 该论文提出InfoDensity奖励框架，通过优化推理质量而非单纯缩短长度，在保持准确率的同时显著减少LLM推理过程中的token使用量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法仅优化最终响应长度，忽视了中间推理步骤的质量，导致模型容易受到奖励攻击。作者认为冗余性不仅是长度问题，更是中间推理质量低下的表现。

Method: 提出InfoDensity奖励框架，结合基于AUC的奖励和单调性奖励作为推理质量的统一度量，并通过长度缩放项鼓励用更简洁的方式达到同等质量。

Result: 在数学推理基准测试中，InfoDensity在准确率上匹配或超越现有最佳方法，同时显著减少token使用量，实现了良好的准确率-效率权衡。

Conclusion: 高质量推理轨迹具有信息密集特性，InfoDensity通过优化推理质量而非单纯压缩长度，有效解决了LLM推理冗余问题。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) with extended reasoning capabilities often generate verbose and redundant reasoning traces, incurring unnecessary computational cost. While existing reinforcement learning approaches address this by optimizing final response length, they neglect the quality of intermediate reasoning steps, leaving models vulnerable to reward hacking. We argue that verbosity is not merely a length problem, but a symptom of poor intermediate reasoning quality. To investigate this, we conduct an empirical study tracking the conditional entropy of the answer distribution across reasoning steps. We find that high-quality reasoning traces exhibit two consistent properties: low uncertainty convergence and monotonic progress. These findings suggest that high-quality reasoning traces are informationally dense, that is, each step contributes meaningful entropy reduction relative to the total reasoning length. Motivated by this, we propose InfoDensity, a reward framework for RL training that combines an AUC-based reward and a monotonicity reward as a unified measure of reasoning quality, weighted by a length scaling term that favors achieving equivalent quality more concisely. Experiments on mathematical reasoning benchmarks demonstrate that InfoDensity matches or surpasses state-of-the-art baselines in accuracy while significantly reducing token usage, achieving a strong accuracy-efficiency trade-off.

Validated on one full year (2023) of AIS data across seven Gulf of Mexico routes (840 episodes per method), PIER reduces mean CO2 emissions by 10% relative to great-circle routing. However, PIER's primary contribution is eliminating catastrophic fuel waste: great-circle routing incurs extreme fuel consumption (>1.5x median) in 4.8% of voyages; PIER reduces this to 0.5%, a 9-fold reduction. Per-voyage fuel variance is 3.5x lower (p<0.001), with bootstrap 95% CI for mean savings [2.9%, 15.7%]. Crucially, PIER is forecast-independent: unlike A* path optimization whose wave protection degrades 4.5x under realistic forecast uncertainty, PIER maintains constant performance using only local observations. This observation motivates us to consider encouraging LRMs to make safety decisions before CoT generation. To this end, we propose a novel safety alignment method that promotes the safety decision-making of LRMs before starting CoT generation. Specifically, we first utilize a Bert-based classifier to extract safety decision signals from a safe model (e.g., a CoT-disabled LRM) and then integrate these signals into LRMs' safety alignment as auxiliary supervision. In this way, the safety gradients can be backpropagated to the LRMs' latent representations, effectively strengthening the LRMs' safety decision-making abilities against CoT generation. Extensive experiments demonstrate that our method substantially improves the safety capabilities of LRMs while effectively maintaining LRMs' general reasoning performance.

These pilot results do not establish clinical generalization; rather, they suggest that proactive inquiry may be methodologically interesting under tightly controlled conditions and can be viewed as a conceptually appealing formulation worth further investigation for dialogue-based EMR generation. This work should be read as a pilot concept demonstration under a controlled simulated setting rather than as evidence of clinical deployment readiness. ### [199] [Informative Semi-Factuals for XAI: The Elaborated Explanations that People Prefer](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17534)
*Saugat Aryal,Mark T. Keane*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的可解释AI方法——信息性半事实解释（ISF），它不仅生成半事实解释（说明即使改变某些特征预测结果仍保持不变），还补充了影响自动化决策的隐藏特征信息，从而提供更丰富的解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前半事实解释方法虽然能说明即使改变某些输入特征预测结果仍保持不变，但无法解释为什么这些极端值变化不会改变结果。例如，在银行贷款场景中，现有方法只能告诉用户"即使贷款金额翻倍，申请仍会被批准"，但无法解释为什么可以这样，比如是因为用户信用评分高。这种解释的不足促使研究者开发更信息丰富的半事实解释方法。

Method: 本文提出了一种新算法——信息性半事实解释（ISF）方法。该方法不仅生成传统的半事实解释（找到不改变预测结果的单个关键特征的最大值变化），还补充了关于影响自动化决策的额外隐藏特征的信息。ISF通过识别和解释那些使极端值变化不会改变结果的底层因素，为半事实解释增加了信息深度。

Result: 在基准数据集上的实验结果表明，ISF方法生成的半事实解释既信息丰富，又在关键指标上具有高质量。用户研究进一步显示，人们更喜欢这种经过详细阐述的解释，而不是当前方法生成的简单半事实解释。

Conclusion: 信息性半事实解释（ISF）方法通过补充隐藏特征信息，显著提升了半事实解释的信息价值和实用性，为用户提供了更深入、更有意义的解释，有助于增强对AI决策的理解和信任。

Abstract: Recently, in eXplainable AI (XAI), $\textit{even if}$ explanations -- so-called semi-factuals -- have emerged as a popular strategy that explains how a predicted outcome $\textit{can remain the same}$ even when certain input-features are altered. For example, in the commonly-used banking app scenario, a semi-factual explanation could inform customers about better options, other alternatives for their successful application, by saying "$\textit{Even if}$ you asked for double the loan amount, you would still be accepted". Most semi-factuals XAI algorithms focus on finding maximal value-changes to a single key-feature that do $\textit{not}$ alter the outcome (unlike counterfactual explanations that often find minimal value-changes to several features that alter the outcome). However, no current semi-factual method explains $\textit{why}$ these extreme value-changes do not alter outcomes; for example, a more informative semi-factual could tell the customer that it is their good credit score that allows them to borrow double their requested loan. In this work, we advance a new algorithm -- the $\textit{informative semi-factuals}$ (ISF) method -- that generates more elaborated explanations supplementing semi-factuals with information about additional $\textit{hidden features}$ that influence an automated decision. Experimental results on benchmark datasets show that this ISF method computes semi-factuals that are both informative and of high-quality on key metrics. Furthermore, a user study shows that people prefer these elaborated explanations over the simpler semi-factual explanations generated by current methods.

</details>


### [200] [Sensi: Learn One Thing at a Time -- Curriculum-Based Test-Time Learning for LLM Game Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17683)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体在未知环境中需要数千次交互才能形成有用假设，学习效率低下，需要更有效的测试时学习方法。

Method: 采用三机制架构：1) 感知与动作分离的双玩家架构；2) 外部状态机管理的课程学习系统；3) 数据库作为控制平面实现可编程上下文窗口。还包含LLM作为裁判的动态评估机制。

Result: Sensi v1解决了2个游戏关卡，Sensi v2虽然未解决任何关卡，但仅用约32次尝试就完成了整个学习课程，相比需要1600-3000次尝试的系统实现了50-94倍的样本效率提升。

Conclusion: 架构瓶颈已从学习效率转移到感知基础问题，这是一个更易处理的问题。感知层的自洽幻觉级联是主要失败模式，表明需要改进感知基础。

Abstract: Large language model (LLM) agents deployed in unknown environments must learn task structure at test time, but current approaches require thousands of interactions to form useful hypotheses. We present Sensi, an LLM agent architecture for the ARC-AGI-3 game-playing challenge that introduces structured test-time learning through three mechanisms: (1) a two-player architecture separating perception from action, (2) a curriculum-based learning system managed by an external state machine, and (3) a database-as-control-plane that makes the agents context window programmatically steerable. We further introduce an LLM-as-judge component with dynamically generated evaluation rubrics to determine when the agent has learned enough about one topic to advance to the next. We report results across two iterations: Sensi v1 solves 2 game levels using the two-player architecture alone, while Sensi v2 adds curriculum learning and solves 0 levels - but completes its entire learning curriculum in approximately 32 action attempts, achieving 50-94x greater sample efficiency than comparable systems that require 1600-3000 attempts. We precisely diagnose the failure mode as a self-consistent hallucination cascade originating in the perception layer, demonstrating that the architectural bottleneck has shifted from learning efficiency to perceptual grounding - a more tractable problem.

</details>


### [201] [MALLES: A Multi-agent LLMs-based Economic Sandbox with Consumer Preference Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17694)
*Yusen Wu,Yiran Liu,Xiaotie Deng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: MALLES：基于多智能体大语言模型的经济沙盒，通过偏好学习和均值场机制解决高维多模态环境下的决策模拟问题，提升产品选择和购买预测的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现实经济中的决策面临高维多模态环境、智能体异质性和组合数据稀疏性等挑战，需要建立统一、可扩展的仿真框架来支持跨领域、跨类别的经济决策分析。

Method: 1. 偏好学习范式：通过对多样化产品类别的大规模异质交易记录进行后训练，使LLM经济对齐并内化消费者偏好模式；2. 均值场机制：建模产品环境与客户群体间的动态交互，稳定高维决策空间的采样过程；3. 多智能体讨论框架：通过专业化智能体协作处理大量产品信息，分散认知负荷并捕捉关键决策因素。

Result: 相比现有经济和金融LLM模拟基准，该框架在产品选择准确性、购买数量预测和模拟稳定性方面取得显著提升，验证了大语言模型作为高保真、可扩展决策模拟基础支柱的潜力。

Conclusion: MALLES框架通过结合偏好学习、均值场稳定机制和多智能体协作，有效解决了经济决策模拟中的数据稀疏性和高维复杂性挑战，为基于基础数据库的现实经济分析提供了可行的技术路径。

Abstract: In the real economy, modern decision-making is fundamentally challenged by high-dimensional, multimodal environments, which are further complicated by agent heterogeneity and combinatorial data sparsity. This paper introduces a Multi-Agent Large Language Model-based Economic Sandbox (MALLES), leveraging the inherent generalization capabilities of large-sacle models to establish a unified simulation framework applicable to cross-domain and cross-category scenarios. Central to our approach is a preference learning paradigm in which LLMs are economically aligned via post-training on extensive, heterogeneous transaction records across diverse product categories. This methodology enables the models to internalize and transfer latent consumer preference patterns, thereby mitigating the data sparsity issues prevalent in individual categories. To enhance simulation stability, we implement a mean-field mechanism designed to model the dynamic interactions between the product environment and customer populations, effectively stabilizing sampling processes within high-dimensional decision spaces. Furthermore, we propose a multi-agent discussion framework wherein specialized agents collaboratively process extensive product information. This architecture distributes cognitive load to alleviate single-agent attention bottlenecks and captures critical decision factors through structured dialogue. Experiments demonstrate that our framework achieves significant improvements in product selection accuracy, purchase quantity prediction, and simulation stability compared to existing economic and financial LLM simulation baselines. Our results substantiate the potential of large language models as a foundational pillar for high-fidelity, scalable decision simulation and latter analysis in the real economy based on foundational database.

</details>


### [202] [From Virtual Environments to Real-World Trials: Emerging Trends in Autonomous Driving](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17714)
*A. Humnabadkar,A. Sikdar,B. Cave,H. Zhang,N. Bessis,A. Behera*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文综述了自动驾驶、仿真技术和合成数据的最新进展，重点分析了合成数据在感知规划、数字孪生验证和域适应策略三个核心维度的应用，并探讨了未来研究方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 自动驾驶技术的实际部署面临数据稀缺、安全要求和跨环境泛化等挑战，而合成数据和虚拟环境提供了可扩展、可控且标注丰富的训练评估场景，成为解决这些问题的关键途径。

Method: 从三个核心维度组织研究现状：(1)合成数据在感知和规划中的应用；(2)基于数字孪生的系统验证仿真；(3)连接合成与现实数据的域适应策略。同时分析了视觉语言模型和仿真真实感在增强场景理解和泛化中的作用，提供了数据集、工具和仿真平台的详细分类。

Result: 建立了自动驾驶仿真和合成数据研究的系统框架，总结了当前技术发展现状，识别了关键趋势和挑战，为研究者提供了全面的技术路线图。

Conclusion: 合成数据和仿真技术是加速自动驾驶发展的关键，但需要解决Sim2Real迁移、可扩展安全验证、协同自主和仿真驱动策略学习等核心挑战，才能实现安全、可泛化且全球可部署的自动驾驶系统。

Abstract: Autonomous driving technologies have achieved significant advances in recent years, yet their real-world deployment remains constrained by data scarcity, safety requirements, and the need for generalization across diverse environments. In response, synthetic data and virtual environments have emerged as powerful enablers, offering scalable, controllable, and richly annotated scenarios for training and evaluation. This survey presents a comprehensive review of recent developments at the intersection of autonomous driving, simulation technologies, and synthetic datasets. We organize the landscape across three core dimensions: (i) the use of synthetic data for perception and planning, (ii) digital twin-based simulation for system validation, and (iii) domain adaptation strategies bridging synthetic and real-world data. We also highlight the role of vision-language models and simulation realism in enhancing scene understanding and generalization. A detailed taxonomy of datasets, tools, and simulation platforms is provided, alongside an analysis of trends in benchmark design. Finally, we discuss critical challenges and open research directions, including Sim2Real transfer, scalable safety validation, cooperative autonomy, and simulation-driven policy learning, that must be addressed to accelerate the path toward safe, generalizable, and globally deployable autonomous driving systems.

### [203] [Facts as First Class Objects: Knowledge Objects for Persistent LLM Memory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17781)
*Oliver Zahn,Simran Chana*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文对比了上下文记忆与知识对象两种知识存储方式，发现上下文记忆存在容量限制、压缩损失和目标漂移三大问题，而知识对象在准确性、成本和推理能力方面表现更优。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随着大型语言模型越来越多地作为持久知识工作者使用，上下文记忆成为默认策略。然而，这种策略在实际部署中存在严重缺陷，需要探索更可靠的知识存储和检索方法。

Method: 通过基准测试对比上下文记忆与知识对象（KOs）的性能。知识对象采用离散哈希寻址元组，具有O(1)检索复杂度。测试包括准确性、成本、多跳推理能力，并在四个前沿模型上进行跨模型验证。

Result: 上下文记忆在7000个事实内可达100%准确率，但存在三大失败模式：容量限制（8000个事实时提示溢出）、压缩损失（摘要破坏60%事实）、目标漂移（级联压缩侵蚀54%项目约束）。知识对象在所有条件下保持100%准确率，成本降低252倍，多跳推理准确率达78.9%（vs 31.6%）。

Conclusion: 上下文记忆存在根本性架构缺陷，而知识对象提供更可靠、高效的知识存储方案。研究还发现嵌入检索在对抗性事实上表现不佳，神经记忆存储事实但无法按需检索。提出了密度自适应检索作为切换机制，并发布了基准测试套件。

Abstract: Large language models increasingly serve as persistent knowledge workers, with in-context memory - facts stored in the prompt - as the default strategy. We benchmark in-context memory against Knowledge Objects (KOs), discrete hash-addressed tuples with O(1) retrieval. Within the context window, Claude Sonnet 4.5 achieves 100% exact-match accuracy from 10 to 7,000 facts (97.5% of its 200K window). However, production deployment reveals three failure modes: capacity limits (prompts overflow at 8,000 facts), compaction loss (summarization destroys 60% of facts), and goal drift (cascading compaction erodes 54% of project constraints while the model continues with full confidence). KOs achieve 100% accuracy across all conditions at 252x lower cost. On multi-hop reasoning, KOs reach 78.9% versus 31.6% for in-context. Cross-model replication across four frontier models confirms compaction loss is architectural, not model-specific. We additionally show that embedding retrieval fails on adversarial facts (20% precision at 1) and that neural memory (Titans) stores facts but fails to retrieve them on demand. We introduce density-adaptive retrieval as a switching mechanism and release the benchmark suite.

</details>


### [204] [RPMS: Enhancing LLM-Based Embodied Planning through Rule-Augmented Memory Synergy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.17831)
*Zhenhang Yuan,Shenghai Yuan,Lihua Xie*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: RPMS架构通过规则检索和信念状态管理，解决了LLM智能体在封闭世界环境中的动作无效和状态漂移问题，显著提升了任务成功率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM智能体在封闭世界具身环境中经常失败，因为动作需要满足严格的前提条件（如位置、库存、容器状态），而失败反馈稀疏。研究者识别了两种结构性耦合的失败模式：无效动作生成和状态漂移，它们相互放大形成退化循环。

Method: 提出了RPMS（冲突管理架构），通过结构化规则检索强制执行动作可行性，通过轻量级信念状态门控记忆适用性，并通过规则优先仲裁解决两个来源之间的冲突。

Result: 在ALFWorld的134个未见任务中，RPMS使用Llama 3.1 8B实现了59.7%的单次试验成功率（比基线提高23.9个百分点），使用Claude Sonnet 4.5达到98.5%（提高11.9个百分点）。规则检索单独贡献了14.9个百分点的提升。在ScienceWorld中，RPMS在所有消融条件下都获得了持续增益（平均得分54.0 vs. ReAct基线的44.9）。

Conclusion: RPMS架构通过规则检索和信念状态管理有效解决了LLM智能体的动作无效和状态漂移问题。关键发现是情景记忆有条件地有用：在没有基础的情况下使用会损害某些任务类型的性能，但一旦通过当前状态过滤并受显式动作规则约束，就会成为稳定的净收益。该架构在不同结构环境间具有可迁移性。

Abstract: LLM agents often fail in closed-world embodied environments because actions must satisfy strict preconditions -- such as location, inventory, and container states -- and failure feedback is sparse. We identify two structurally coupled failure modes: (P1) invalid action generation and (P2) state drift, each amplifying the other in a degenerative cycle. We present RPMS, a conflict-managed architecture that enforces action feasibility via structured rule retrieval, gates memory applicability via a lightweight belief state, and resolves conflicts between the two sources via rules-first arbitration. On ALFWorld (134 unseen tasks), RPMS achieves 59.7% single-trial success with Llama 3.1 8B (+23.9 pp over baseline) and 98.5% with Claude Sonnet 4.5 (+11.9 pp); of the 8B gain, rule retrieval alone contributes +14.9 pp (statistically significant), making it the dominant factor. A key finding is that episodic memory is conditionally useful: it harms performance on some task types when used without grounding, but becomes a stable net positive once filtered by current state and constrained by explicit action rules. Adapting RPMS to ScienceWorld with GPT-4 yields consistent gains across all ablation conditions (avg. score 54.0 vs. 44.9 for the ReAct baseline), providing transfer evidence that the core mechanisms hold across structurally distinct environments.

</details>


### [205] [AgentFactory: A Self-Evolving Framework Through Executable Subagent Accumulation and Reuse](https://arxiv.org/abs/2603.18000)
*Zhang Zhang,Shuqi Lu,Hongjin Qian,Di He,Zheng Liu*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: AgentFactory提出了一种新的LLM智能体自我进化范式，将成功任务解决方案保存为可执行的子智能体代码而非文本经验，实现持续能力积累


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有LLM智能体自我进化方法主要将成功经验记录为文本提示或反思，在复杂场景中无法可靠保证任务高效重新执行，需要更可靠的解决方案保存机制

Method: 提出AgentFactory范式，将成功任务解决方案保存为可执行的子智能体Python代码，基于执行反馈持续精炼这些子智能体，使其随着遇到更多任务而变得更稳健高效

Result: AgentFactory实现了持续能力积累：其可执行子智能体库随时间增长和改进，逐步减少类似任务所需的工作量而无需人工干预，子智能体具有标准化文档和跨Python系统的可移植性

Conclusion: AgentFactory通过将成功经验编码为可执行子智能体而非文本记录，提供了一种更可靠的LLM智能体自我进化方法，支持持续能力积累和跨系统可移植性

Abstract: Building LLM-based agents has become increasingly important. Recent works on LLM-based agent self-evolution primarily record successful experiences as textual prompts or reflections, which cannot reliably guarantee efficient task re-execution in complex scenarios. We propose AgentFactory, a new self-evolution paradigm that preserves successful task solutions as executable subagent code rather than textual experience. Crucially, these subagents are continuously refined based on execution feedback, becoming increasingly robust and efficient as more tasks are encountered. Saved subagents are pure Python code with standardized documentation, enabling portability across any Python-capable system. We demonstrate that AgentFactory enables continuous capability accumulation: its library of executable subagents grows and improves over time, progressively reducing the effort required for similar tasks without manual intervention. Our implementation is open-sourced at https://github.com/zzatpku/AgentFactory, and our demonstration video is available at https://youtu.be/iKSsuAXJHW0.

</details>
